Captain Rufus W. Beaujean diary, 1888		Beaujean, Rufus W.			Diary on 19th Century Community Development in Florida authored by town developer, carpenter, handyman, and Civil War veteran Capt. Rufus W. Beaujean of Melbourne Beach in Brevard County, Florida.  The diary provides details of the many aspects of his work helping neighbors, and socializing with, and executing chores for named male and female residents. Richard Call letter draft to George Graham, March 20, 1830		Call, Richard Keith, 1791-1862			Investigating the Spanish land grants: draft of a letter in which Call reported on his mission to Havana as assistant U.S. counsel in the cases of the Arrendondo and Forbes land grants made by Spain prior to cession. After some lengthy litigation the government would eventually lose, Call has here claimed success in his efforts to discredit some of the grants to influential traders in accordance with American aims. His letter goes to the heart of the subject of land ownership that has in one way or another always been vitally connected with the state's history and very existence.
